<h1 class="firstHeading mw-first-heading" id="firstHeading"><span class="mw-page-title-main">直线</span></h1>
<div class="vector-body" id="bodyContent">
<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">维基百科，自由的百科全书</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div id="contentSub2"></div>
<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">跳到导航</a>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">跳到搜索</a>
<div class="mw-body-content mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="zh"><div class="mw-parser-output"><table class="box-Unreferenced plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Tango-nosources.svg"><img alt="Tango-nosources.svg" data-file-height="48" data-file-width="48" decoding="async" height="45" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4e/Tango-nosources.svg/45px-Tango-nosources.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4e/Tango-nosources.svg/68px-Tango-nosources.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4e/Tango-nosources.svg/90px-Tango-nosources.svg.png 2x" width="45"/></a></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><span class="mbox-text-span">此條目<b>没有列出任何<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E5%88%97%E6%98%8E%E6%9D%A5%E6%BA%90" title="Wikipedia:列明来源">参考或来源</a></b>。<span class="hide-when-compact"></span> <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">2009年7月21日</span>)</i></small><span class="hide-when-compact"><br/><small>維基百科所有的內容都應該<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E5%8F%AF%E4%BE%9B%E6%9F%A5%E8%AD%89" title="Wikipedia:可供查證">可供查證</a>。请协助補充<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E5%8F%AF%E9%9D%A0%E6%9D%A5%E6%BA%90" title="Wikipedia:可靠来源">可靠来源</a>以<a class="external text" href="https://zh.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=%E7%9B%B4%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit">改善这篇条目</a>。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E5%8F%AF%E4%BE%9B%E6%9F%A5%E8%AF%81" title="Wikipedia:可供查证">无法查证</a>的內容可能會因為異議提出而移除。</small></span><span class="hide-when-compact"></span></span></td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Linear_functions2.PNG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="403" data-file-width="402" decoding="async" height="301" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Linear_functions2.PNG/300px-Linear_functions2.PNG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/8/80/Linear_functions2.PNG 1.5x" width="300"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Linear_functions2.PNG" title="放大"></a></div>三条直线：紅線與藍線有相同的斜率, 紅線與綠線有相同的<i>y</i>-<a href="/wiki/%E6%88%AA%E8%B7%9D" title="截距">截距</a> 。</div></div></div>
<p><b>直線</b>，是一個點在<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E9%9D%A2_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="平面 (数学)">平面</a>或<a href="/wiki/%E7%A9%BA%E9%96%93" title="空間">空間</a>沿著一定方向和其相反方向運動的軌跡，是不彎曲的線。直線是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B9%BE%E4%BD%95%E5%AD%B8" title="幾何學">幾何學</a>的基本概念，在不同的幾何學體系中有著不同的描述。在這裡主要描述<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AD%90%E5%B9%BE%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%97%E7%A9%BA%E9%96%93" title="歐幾里得空間">歐幾里得空間</a>中的直線。其他<a href="/wiki/%E6%9B%B2%E7%8E%87" title="曲率">曲率</a>非零狀況下的直線，請參考<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9D%9E%E6%AD%90%E5%B9%BE%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%97%E5%B9%BE%E4%BD%95" title="非歐幾里得幾何">非歐幾里得幾何</a>。
</p><p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AD%90%E5%B9%BE%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%97%E5%B9%BE%E4%BD%95" title="歐幾里得幾何">歐幾里得幾何</a>研究<a href="/wiki/%E6%9B%B2%E7%8E%87" title="曲率">曲率</a>為零的空間下狀況，它並未對點、直線、平面、空間給出定義，而是通過公理來描述點線面的關係。
<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AD%90%E5%B9%BE%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%97%E5%B9%BE%E4%BD%95" title="歐幾里得幾何">歐幾里得幾何</a>中的直線可以看作是一個點的集合，這個集合中的任意一點都在這個集合中的其他任意兩點所確定的直綫上。
</p><p>“過兩點有且只有一條直線”是歐幾里得幾何體系中的一條<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%AC%E7%90%86" title="公理">公理</a>，“有且只有”意即“確定”，即兩點確定一直線。
</p><p>在幾何學中，直線沒有粗細，沒有端點，沒有方向性，具有無限的長度，具有固定的位置。
</p>
<div aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading" class="toc" id="toc" role="navigation"><input class="toctogglecheckbox" id="toctogglecheckbox" role="button" style="display:none" type="checkbox"/><div class="toctitle" dir="ltr" lang="zh"><h2 id="mw-toc-heading">目录</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>

<h2><span id=".E7.B7.9A.E6.80.A7.E6.96.B9.E7.A8.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="線性方程">線性方程</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9B%B4%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：線性方程">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B7%9A%E6%80%A7%E6%96%B9%E7%A8%8B" title="線性方程">線性方程</a></div>
<p>在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A7%A3%E6%9E%90%E5%B9%BE%E4%BD%95" title="解析幾何">解析幾何</a>中，我們常用<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B7%9A%E6%80%A7%E6%96%B9%E7%A8%8B" title="線性方程">線性方程</a>描述一條直線。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E4.BA.8C.E7.B6.AD.E7.9B.B4.E8.A7.92.E5.9D.90.E6.A8.99.E7.B3.BB.E6.96.B9.E7.A8.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="二維直角坐標系方程">二維直角坐標系方程</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9B%B4%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：二維直角坐標系方程">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>平行於<i>x</i>-或<i>y</i>-軸</b>
</p><p>最簡單的直線方程是平行於<i>x</i>-軸或<i>y</i>-軸的直線：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x=a\;}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mspace width="thickmathspace"></mspace>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x=a\;}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle x=a\;}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a78991ea0f21f5f1592f3f54163e869b8edf92e9" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.303ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> 或 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \;y=b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \;y=b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \;y=b}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/038052806c077e39ea5c7ee66bb958b301210c5a" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:5.897ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>，</dd></dl>
<p>當中 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> 和 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 分別是<i>x</i>-和<i>y</i>-截距。
</p><p><b>一般式</b>
</p><p>對於所有的直線，都可以形式
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle Ax+By+C=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mi>y</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>C</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle Ax+By+C=0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="Ax+By+C=0" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9e84e63a5c044f46835839af53ccbe7a695187da" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:17.7ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>來表示。
</p><p>這表示示形式並不是唯一的，但習慣上常限制 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\geq 0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>≥<!-- ≥ --></mo>
<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\geq 0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A\geq 0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ebee3e714a32508aa26658d5c88f6a09237c82dc" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:6.004ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span> 及 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \gcd(A,B,C)=1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo form="prefix" movablelimits="true">gcd</mo>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mi>C</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \gcd(A,B,C)=1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \gcd(A,B,C)=1}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8941e385c6ffe7dfb075a56af102a2e84682bcb4" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:16.899ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span> 。在此限制下，同一條直線只有一種表達形式。
</p><p>在這形式下，直線的斜率是 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle -{\frac {A}{B}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mi>A</mi>
<mi>B</mi>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle -{\frac {A}{B}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle -{\frac {A}{B}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f02d808d986f9bf848ab712dce47974df1e08118" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:4.408ex; height:5.343ex;"/></span> ，<i>x</i>-截距是 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle -{\frac {C}{A}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle -{\frac {C}{A}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/09247ad3cb2846025063b20191d6ae130d5aef16" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:4.411ex; height:5.509ex;"/></span> ，<i>y</i>-截距是 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle -{\frac {C}{B}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<mi>C</mi>
<mi>B</mi>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle -{\frac {C}{B}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle -{\frac {C}{B}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/690f53d6dfce6e55fad6b68821975a2ab9dd7548" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:4.411ex; height:5.343ex;"/></span> 。
</p><p><b>斜截式</b>
</p><p>在直線不平行於<i>y</i>-軸時，若斜率是 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle m}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>m</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle m}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle m}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0a07d98bb302f3856cbabc47b2b9016692e3f7bc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.04ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> ，<i>y</i>-截距是 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> ，則有方程
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle y=mx+b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>在這形式下，直線的表達形式是唯一的。
</p><p><b>二點式</b>

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle y-y_{0}=m\,(x-x_{0})}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p><b>截距式</b>
</p><p>若直線的<i>x</i>-和<i>y</i>-截距分別是 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> 和 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> ，則方程為
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {x \over a}+{y \over b}=1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<mi>a</mi>
</mfrac>
</mrow>

<mi>y</mi>
<mi>b</mi>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {x \over a}+{y \over b}=1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{x \over a}+{y \over b}=1" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/09becc7be75a4b28c69f2efb78dd556443afd3fd" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:11.259ex; height:5.009ex;"/></span>。</dd></dl>
<p><b>法線式</b>
</p><p>過原點向直線作一垂直線段，若該線長度為 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>p</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle p}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="p" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/81eac1e205430d1f40810df36a0edffdc367af36" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:1.259ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span> ，且與正<i>x</i>-軸的傾斜角為 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \alpha }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x\cos \alpha +y\sin \alpha -p=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>

<h3><span id=".E4.B8.89.E7.B6.AD.E7.9B.B4.E8.A7.92.E5.9D.90.E6.A8.99.E7.B3.BB.E6.96.B9.E7.A8.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="三維直角坐標系方程">三維直角坐標系方程</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9B%B4%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：三維直角坐標系方程">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>在三維坐標上，由於一條等式只代表一個平面，一條直線須由最少兩條等式定義。
</p><p><b>平行於<i>x</i>-、<i>y</i>-或<i>z</i>-軸</b>

</p>

<p>的形式。
</p><p><b>一般式</b>
</p><p>對於任何直線，一般式都能以兩個非<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E8%A1%8C" title="平行">平行</a>平面定義：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\begin{alignedat}{9}A_{1}x&amp;&amp;\;+\;&amp;&amp;B_{1}y&amp;&amp;\;+\;&amp;&amp;C_{1}z\;&amp;&amp;+\;&amp;&amp;D_{1}\;&amp;&amp;=\;&amp;&amp;0&amp;\\A_{2}x&amp;&amp;\;+\;&amp;&amp;B_{2}y&amp;&amp;\;+\;&amp;&amp;C_{2}z\;&amp;&amp;+\;&amp;&amp;D_{2}\;&amp;&amp;=\;&amp;&amp;0\end{alignedat}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<p>其中 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A_{1}:B_{1}:C_{1}\neq A_{2}:B_{2}:C_{2}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A_{1}:B_{1}:C_{1}\neq A_{2}:B_{2}:C_{2}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A_{1}:B_{1}:C_{1}\neq A_{2}:B_{2}:C_{2}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e5913b95ec674c5e2466d08fb3c41974dfe12f99" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:27.51ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span> 。
</p><p>由於從一條直線可引申出無限對平面，這表示方式並不是唯一的。因此又能考慮以三個<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%B1%E7%B7%9A_(%E5%B9%BE%E4%BD%95)" title="共線 (幾何)">共線</a>平面定義：
</p>

<p>或合併記作
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle Ax-By+D=Cy-Az+E=Bz-Cx+F=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>其中係數須乎合關係 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle AF+BE+CD=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mi>F</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mi>E</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>C</mi>
<mi>D</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle AF+BE+CD=0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle AF+BE+CD=0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/96b6cd2a7bf1bdf3ff29bc699276175758984d3c" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:20.656ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span> ，以保證三個平面相交於同一直線。
</p><p>事實上，這三條等式分別對應著直線在<i>xy</i>-、<i>yz</i>-和<i>xz</i>-平面的投影。
</p><p>在限制 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\geq 0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>≥<!-- ≥ --></mo>
<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\geq 0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A\geq 0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ebee3e714a32508aa26658d5c88f6a09237c82dc" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:6.004ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span> 及 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \gcd(A,B,C,D,E,F)=1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \gcd(A,B,C,D,E,F)=1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \gcd(A,B,C,D,E,F)=1}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/fad5a1be1f7eb757d0f53275cadc1140d31329bc" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:25.441ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span> 下，同一條直線只有一種表達形式。
</p><p>（注：對於平行於軸平面的直線，例如 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 2y-3z+1=x-1=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mn>1</mn>

<mn>0</mn>

</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 2y-3z+1=x-1=0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0cbaf2145aa88c7647cf8e40f20ad9809086274e" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:24.104ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> ，會有以下表示方式：
</p>

<p>對於定義一條直線，這步驟是非必要的。但在本頁往後的部份，這表示方式能簡化一些公式。）
</p><p><b>斜截式</b>

<mi>λ<!-- λ --></mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="bold">u</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbf {r} =\mathbf {a} +\lambda \mathbf {u} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \mathbf {r} =\mathbf {a} +\lambda \mathbf {u} }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/fc54f27abb3b87083307a4df23c9a36b157e5177" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:11.181ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span> ，</dd></dl>
<p>當中 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbf {r} ={\begin{bmatrix}x\\y\\z\\\end{bmatrix}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="bold">r</mi>
</mrow>
<mo>=</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mrow>
<mo>[</mo>
<mtable columnspacing="1em" rowspacing="4pt">
<mtr>

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbf {r} ={\begin{bmatrix}x\\y\\z\\\end{bmatrix}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \mathbf {r} ={\begin{bmatrix}x\\y\\z\\\end{bmatrix}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/72134953a281d58665e45b7677597538d4a430f9" style="vertical-align: -4.171ex; width:9.382ex; height:9.509ex;"/></span> ，而 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \lambda }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>須要注意的是，這直線的表達形式並不是唯一的。
</p><p><b>參數式</b>
</p><p>從向量式出發，可以參數 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \lambda }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>

<h2><span id=".E7.9B.B4.E7.B7.9A.E8.88.87.E8.A7.A3.E6.9E.90.E5.B9.BE.E4.BD.95"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="直線與解析幾何">直線與解析幾何</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9B%B4%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：直線與解析幾何">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E9.BB.9E.E8.88.87.E7.9B.B4.E7.B7.9A.E7.9A.84.E8.B7.9D.E9.9B.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="點與直線的距離">點與直線的距離</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9B%B4%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：點與直線的距離">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>一般情況下，點與直线的距离，是指點到直線的最短距離，即<a href="/wiki/%E5%9E%82%E7%9B%B4" title="垂直">垂直</a>距離。
</p><p>在二維直角坐標中，直線 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle Ax+By+C=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

<mi>x</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mi>y</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>C</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle Ax+By+C=0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="Ax+By+C=0" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9e84e63a5c044f46835839af53ccbe7a695187da" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:17.7ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 與點 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (p,q)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle d={\frac {\left|Ap+Bq+C\right|}{\sqrt {A^{2}+B^{2}}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>給出向量式 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbf {r} =\mathbf {a} +\lambda \mathbf {u} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>在三維直角坐標中，直線 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\begin{alignedat}{7}Ax&amp;&amp;\;-\;&amp;&amp;By&amp;&amp;\;+\;&amp;&amp;D\;&amp;&amp;=\;&amp;&amp;0&amp;\\Cy&amp;&amp;\;-\;&amp;&amp;Az&amp;&amp;\;+\;&amp;&amp;E\;&amp;&amp;=\;&amp;&amp;0&amp;\\Bz&amp;&amp;\;-\;&amp;&amp;Cx&amp;&amp;\;+\;&amp;&amp;F\;&amp;&amp;=\;&amp;&amp;0\end{alignedat}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle d={\sqrt {\frac {(Ap-Bq+D)^{2}+(Cq-Ar+E)^{2}+(Br-Cp+F)^{2}}{A^{2}+B^{2}+C^{2}}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>給出向量式 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbf {r} =\mathbf {a} +\lambda \mathbf {u} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h3><span id=".E4.B8.A4.E6.9D.A1.E7.9B.B8.E4.BA.A4.E7.9B.B4.E7.BA.BF.E7.9A.84.E7.9B.B8.E4.BA.A4.E9.BB.9E"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="两条相交直线的相交點">两条相交直线的相交點</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9B%B4%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：两条相交直线的相交點">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>不考慮重合的情形，在二維平面中，兩條相交直線可以<a href="/wiki/%E7%9B%B8%E4%BA%A4" title="相交">相交</a>或<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E8%A1%8C" title="平行">平行</a>。
</p><p>給定兩條直线 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A_{1}x+B_{1}y+C_{1}=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>A</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>

<mo>+</mo>
<msub>
<mi>B</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>1</mn>

</msub>

<mo>+</mo>
<msub>
<mi>C</mi>

<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A_{1}x+B_{1}y+C_{1}=0}</annotation>
</semantics>

<semantics>

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A_{1}:B_{1}\neq A_{2}:B_{2}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>當中 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\begin{vmatrix}a&amp;b\\c&amp;d\end{vmatrix}}=ad-bc}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x=-{\frac {\begin{vmatrix}C_{1}&amp;B_{1}\\C_{2}&amp;B_{2}\end{vmatrix}}{\begin{vmatrix}A_{1}&amp;B_{1}\\A_{2}&amp;B_{2}\end{vmatrix}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle y=-{\frac {\begin{vmatrix}A_{1}&amp;C_{1}\\A_{2}&amp;C_{2}\end{vmatrix}}{\begin{vmatrix}A_{1}&amp;B_{1}\\A_{2}&amp;B_{2}\end{vmatrix}}}}</annotation>

<p>在三維空間中，不考慮重合的情形，兩條直線可以<a href="/wiki/%E7%9B%B8%E4%BA%A4" title="相交">相交</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E8%A1%8C" title="平行">平行</a>或<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AD%AA%E6%96%9C" title="歪斜">歪斜</a>（異面）。

<h3><span id=".E4.B8.A4.E6.9D.A1.E7.9B.B8.E4.BA.A4.E7.9B.B4.E7.BA.BF.E7.9A.84.E5.A4.B9.E8.A7.92"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="两条相交直线的夹角">两条相交直线的夹角</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9B%B4%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：两条相交直线的夹角">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>若兩線<a href="/wiki/%E7%9B%B8%E4%BA%A4" title="相交">相交</a>，則會形成<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%BE%E8%A7%92" title="夾角">夾角</a>。兩線之間的夾角，通常指不大於90°的一隻。
</p><p>在二維平面上，給定直线 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle y=mx+b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>y</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>m</mi>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle y=mx+b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="y=mx+b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/25e966621217067985694be3afd6801d7d51c5d8" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:11.462ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> ，該線與<i>x</i>-軸的夾角為
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \tan \theta =\left|m\right|}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mo>=</mo>
<mrow>
<mo>|</mo>
<mi>m</mi>
<mo>|</mo>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \tan \theta =\left|m\right|}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \tan \theta =\left|m\right|}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/671cdc04476edcc195429705217af66a0f89c063" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:11.27ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span> 。</dd></dl>
<p>給定兩條直线 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle y=m_{1}x+b_{1}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle m_{1}m_{2}=-1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>而其他情況，兩線相交所形成的夾角 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \theta }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \tan \theta =\left|{\frac {m_{1}-m_{2}}{1+m_{1}m_{2}}}\right|}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h3><span id=".E4.B8.A4.E6.9D.A1.E7.9B.B4.E7.BA.BF.E7.9A.84.E8.B7.9D.E9.9B.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="两条直线的距離">两条直线的距離</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9B%B4%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：两条直线的距離">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>一般情況下，两条直线的距离，是指最短距離。
</p><p>二維情況下，两条<a href="/wiki/%E7%9B%B8%E4%BA%A4" title="相交">相交</a>直线的距离必然為 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2aae8864a3c1fec9585261791a809ddec1489950" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.162ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 。
</p><p>若有两條<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E8%A1%8C" title="平行">平行</a>直线 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle Ax+By+C_{1}=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mi>y</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<msub>
<mi>C</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle Ax+By+C_{1}=0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle Ax+By+C_{1}=0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6a5b9cd2f8bc97df9c691656e678560fb331726d" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:18.65ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 及 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle Ax+By+C_{2}=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mi>y</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<msub>
<mi>C</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle Ax+By+C_{2}=0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle Ax+By+C_{2}=0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/38b5607d9eb2f2243ad73e408f79b6350f1db7d6" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:18.65ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> ，則有距離
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle d={\frac {\left|C_{1}-C_{2}\right|}{\sqrt {A^{2}+B^{2}}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</semantics>

<p>當中 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\begin{vmatrix}a&amp;b\\c&amp;d\end{vmatrix}}=ad-bc}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>給定歪斜直線向量式 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbf {r} =\mathbf {a_{1}} +\lambda \mathbf {u_{1}} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
